@section Scripts {
    <script>
        var qty       = 1;
        var sizeIndex = 1;   // 0=Nhỏ, 1=Vừa, 2=Lớn (mặc định Vừa)
        var SIZE_DELTA = 7000; // ±7k mỗi bậc so với Vừa
        var basePrice = @(p.IsOnSale && p.SalePrice > 0 ? p.SalePrice : p.Price);

        // Tính giá hiện tại = basePrice + size delta + toppings
        function calcPrice() {
            var sizeDelta = (sizeIndex - 1) * SIZE_DELTA; // -7k / 0 / +7k
            var toppingSum = 0;
            document.querySelectorAll('.topping-check:checked').forEach(function(cb) {
                toppingSum += parseInt(cb.closest('[data-topping-price]').getAttribute('data-topping-price')) || 0;
            });
            return basePrice + sizeDelta + toppingSum;
        }

        function updateTotal() {
            var price   = calcPrice();
            var total   = (price * qty / 1000).toFixed(0) + 'k';
            var unitK   = (price / 1000).toFixed(0) + 'k';
            var el = document.getElementById('addBtnText');
            if (el) el.textContent = 'Thêm Vào Giỏ — ' + total;

            // Flash giá đơn vị
            var priceEl = document.getElementById('priceDisplay');
            if (priceEl) {
                priceEl.textContent = unitK;
                priceEl.classList.remove('price-flash');
                void priceEl.offsetWidth; // reflow
                priceEl.classList.add('price-flash');
            }
        }

        function changeQty(delta) {
            qty = Math.max(1, qty + delta);
            document.getElementById('qtyDisplay').textContent = qty;
            updateTotal();
        }

        function selectSize(btn) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.size-btn').forEach(function(b) {
                b.classList.remove('active');
                b.style.borderColor = 'rgba(162,123,92,0.2)';
                b.style.color = '#3F4E4F';
            });
            btn.classList.add('active');
            btn.style.borderColor = '#A27B5C';
            btn.style.color = '#A27B5C';
            sizeIndex = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-size-index'));
            updateTotal();
        }

        function selectSugar(btn) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.sugar-btn').forEach(function(b) {
                b.classList.remove('active');
                b.style.background = 'transparent';
                b.style.borderColor = 'rgba(162,123,92,0.25)';
                b.style.color = '#3F4E4F';
            });
            btn.classList.add('active');
            btn.style.background = '#A27B5C';
            btn.style.borderColor = '#A27B5C';
            btn.style.color = '#fff';
        }

        function setMainImg(url, thumb) {
            document.getElementById('mainImg').style.backgroundImage = "url('" + url + "')";
            document.querySelectorAll('.thumb').forEach(function(t) {
                t.classList.remove('active'); t.style.borderColor = 'transparent'; t.style.opacity = '0.6';
            });
            thumb.classList.add('active'); thumb.style.borderColor = '#A27B5C'; thumb.style.opacity = '1';
        }

        // ── Thêm vào giỏ hàng (gọi POST thật) ──────────────────
        async function addToCart(productId) {
            var btn = document.getElementById('addToCartBtn');
            btn.disabled = true; btn.style.opacity = '0.7';

            // Lấy sugar
            var sugarBtn = document.querySelector('.sugar-btn.active');
            var sugar    = sugarBtn ? sugarBtn.textContent.trim() : 'Vừa';

            // Lấy toppings đã chọn
            var selectedToppings = [];
            document.querySelectorAll('.topping-check:checked').forEach(function(cb) {
                selectedToppings.push(cb.closest('[data-topping-name]').getAttribute('data-topping-name'));
            });

            // Lấy size
            var sizeBtn = document.querySelector('.size-btn.active');
            var sizeMap = ['S','M','L'];
            var size    = sizeMap[sizeIndex];

            // Ghi chú
            var note = document.getElementById('noteInput')?.value || '';
            var toppingStr = selectedToppings.join(', ');
            if (note) toppingStr = toppingStr ? toppingStr + ' | ' + note : note;

            try {
                const token = document.querySelector('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]')?.value
                           || document.cookie.match(/XSRF-TOKEN=([^;]+)/)?.[1] || '';

                const resp = await fetch('/Cart/Add', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
                        'RequestVerificationToken': token
                    },
                    body: new URLSearchParams({
                        productId: productId,
                        quantity:  qty,
                        size:      size,
                        sugarLevel: sugar,
                        toppings:  toppingStr
                    })
                });

                const data = await resp.json();
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast('✅ Đã thêm vào giỏ hàng!', 'success');
                    // Cập nhật badge giỏ hàng nếu có
                    var badge = document.getElementById('cart-badge') || document.querySelector('[data-cart-count]');
                    if (badge) badge.textContent = data.cartCount;
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Có lỗi xảy ra', 'error');
                }
            } catch(e) {
                showToast('Không thể kết nối. Vui lòng thử lại.', 'error');
            }

            btn.disabled = false; btn.style.opacity = '1';
        }

        function showToast(msg, type) {
            var existing = document.getElementById('detail-toast');
            if (existing) existing.remove();
            var bg   = type === 'success' ? '#3F4E4F' : '#b91c1c';
            var icon = type === 'success' ? 'check_circle' : 'error';
            var t    = document.createElement('div');
            t.id     = 'detail-toast';
            t.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;bottom:1.5rem;right:1.5rem;z-index:9999;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:14px 20px;border-radius:16px;background:'+bg+';color:#fff;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;box-shadow:0 8px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.18);max-width:320px;';
            t.innerHTML = '<span class="material-symbols-outlined" style="font-size:20px;color:#A27B5C;">'+icon+'</span>'+msg+
                '<button onclick="this.parentElement.remove()" style="margin-left:auto;background:none;border:none;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.6);cursor:pointer;"><span class="material-symbols-outlined" style="font-size:18px;">close</span></button>';
            document.body.appendChild(t);
            setTimeout(function() {
                t.style.transition = 'opacity .5s'; t.style.opacity = '0';
                setTimeout(function() { t.remove(); }, 500);
            }, 3500);
        }

        // Thêm AntiForgery token vào trang (cần cho AJAX POST)
        // Nếu không có trong DOM thì fetch sẽ tự dùng cookie
    </script>

    @* Hidden AntiForgery token cho AJAX *@
    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
}

                </div>

                <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;padding:.75rem 1rem;border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:10px;">
                    <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:.6rem;">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined" style="font-size:18px;color:#a27b5c;">local_offer</span>

                            <div style="font-size:.85rem;font-weight:600;color:#2c3639;">Bật khuyến mãi</div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        // ── Khởi tạo khi load ───────────────────────────────
        (function init() {
            // Sync hiddenImageUrl với urlInput
            const hidden   = document.getElementById('hiddenImageUrl');
            const urlInput = document.getElementById('urlInput');
            if (hidden && urlInput && urlInput.value && !hidden.value) {
                hidden.value = urlInput.value;
            }

            // Khởi tạo Sale toggle
            const saleChecked = document.getElementById('toggleSale').checked;
            toggleSaleBox(saleChecked);
            calcSalePrice();
        })();

        // ── Sale toggle ──────────────────────────────────────
        function toggleSaleBox(on) {
            const box    = document.getElementById('saleBox');
            const slider = document.getElementById('saleSlider');
            const thumb  = document.getElementById('saleThumb');
            if (on) {
                box.classList.add('show');
                slider.style.background = '#a27b5c';
                thumb.style.transform = 'translateX(18px)';
            } else {
                box.classList.remove('show');
                slider.style.background = '#e2e8f0';
                thumb.style.transform = 'translateX(0)';
            }
            calcSalePrice();
        }

        function calcSalePrice() {
            const price    = parseFloat(document.getElementById('Price')?.value) || 0;
            const discount = parseFloat(document.getElementById('DiscountPercent')?.value) || 0;
            const el = document.getElementById('salePriceDisplay');
            if (!el) return;
            if (price > 0 && discount > 0) {
                const sale = price * (1 - discount / 100);
                el.textContent = sale.toLocaleString('vi-VN') + '₫';
            } else {
                el.textContent = price > 0 ? price.toLocaleString('vi-VN') + '₫' : '—';
            }
        }

        // ── Ảnh ─────────────────────────────────────────────
        function previewImage(e) {
            const file = e.target.files[0];
            if (!file) return;
            const reader = new FileReader();
            reader.onload = ev => setPreview(ev.target.result);
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
            document.getElementById('hiddenImageUrl').value = '';
            document.getElementById('urlInput').value = '';
        }

        function applyUrlPreview() {
            const url = document.getElementById('urlInput').value.trim();
            document.getElementById('hiddenImageUrl').value = url;
            if (url) setPreview(url);
        }

        function setPreview(src) {
            const el = document.getElementById('imgPreview');
            if (el.tagName === 'IMG') {
                el.src = src;
            } else {
                const img = document.createElement('img');
                img.src = src; img.className = 'ep-img-current'; img.id = 'imgPreview';
                el.replaceWith(img);
            }
        }

        // Drag & drop
        const dz = document.getElementById('dropZone');
        dz.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); dz.style.borderColor='#a27b5c'; });
        dz.addEventListener('dragleave', () => { dz.style.borderColor=''; });
        dz.addEventListener('drop', e => {
            e.preventDefault(); dz.style.borderColor='';
            const file = e.dataTransfer.files[0];
            if (file && file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
                const dt = new DataTransfer(); dt.items.add(file);
                document.getElementById('fileInput').files = dt.files;
                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = ev => setPreview(ev.target.result);
                reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                document.getElementById('hiddenImageUrl').value = '';
            }
        });

        // ── Counter ──────────────────────────────────────────
        function updateCounter(fId, cId, max) {
            document.getElementById(cId).textContent = document.getElementById(fId).value.length;
        }

        // ── Submit với validation ─────────────────────────────
        function submitForm() {
            let valid = true;
            const checks = [
                { id:'Name',       err:'nameErr',  isNum:false },
                { id:'Price',      err:'priceErr', isNum:true  },
                { id:'CategoryId', err:'catErr',   isNum:false },
            ];
            checks.forEach(c => {
                const el    = document.getElementById(c.id);
                const errEl = document.getElementById(c.err);
                const bad   = c.isNum ? (!el.value || parseFloat(el.value) < 0) : !el.value.trim();
                if (bad) { el.classList.add('error'); errEl.classList.add('show'); valid = false; }
                else     { el.classList.remove('error'); errEl.classList.remove('show'); }
            });
            if (!valid) { showToast('⚠ Vui lòng điền đầy đủ thông tin.'); return; }
            document.getElementById('editForm').submit();
        }

        // ── Modal & Toast ─────────────────────────────────────
        function showDeleteModal() { document.getElementById('deleteOverlay').classList.add('show'); }
        function closeModal()      { document.getElementById('deleteOverlay').classList.remove('show'); }
        function showToast(msg) {
            const t = document.getElementById('toast');
            document.getElementById('toastMsg').textContent = msg || 'Đã lưu!';
            t.classList.add('show');
            setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3200);
        }

        @if (TempData["Success"] != null)
        {
                <text>setTimeout(() => showToast('@TempData["Success"]'), 300);</text>
        }
    </script>
}

               onfocus="this.style.borderColor='#a27b5c'" onblur="this.style.borderColor='rgba(162,123,92,.25)'" />
    </div>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:.5rem;flex-wrap:wrap;">
        <button class="pi-filter-btn active" onclick="filterCat(0,this)">Tất Cả</button>
        <button class="pi-filter-btn" onclick="filterCat(1,this)">Trà & Thảo Mộc</button>
        <button class="pi-filter-btn" onclick="filterCat(2,this)">Cà Phê</button>
        <button class="pi-filter-btn" onclick="filterCat(3,this)">Bánh Sáng</button>
    </div>
</div>

                @Html.AntiForgeryToken()

                </button>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        function filterTable() {
            const q = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
            document.querySelectorAll('#productTable tbody tr').forEach(r => {
                r.style.display = (r.dataset.name || '').includes(q) ? '' : 'none';
            });
            updateCount();
        }
        let activeCat = 0;
        function filterCat(cat, btn) {
            activeCat = cat;
            document.querySelectorAll('.pi-filter-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
            btn.classList.add('active');
            document.querySelectorAll('#productTable tbody tr').forEach(r => {
                r.style.display = (cat === 0 || parseInt(r.dataset.cat) === cat) ? '' : 'none';
            });
            updateCount();
        }
        function updateCount() {
            const v = [...document.querySelectorAll('#productTable tbody tr')].filter(r => r.style.display !== 'none').length;
            document.getElementById('rowCount').textContent = v + ' sản phẩm';
            document.getElementById('tableCount').textContent = 'Hiển thị ' + v + ' sản phẩm';
        }
        function showDelete(id, name) {
            document.getElementById('deleteId').value = id;
            document.getElementById('deleteName').textContent = name;
            document.getElementById('deleteForm').action = '/Product/Delete';
            document.getElementById('deleteOverlay').classList.add('show');
        }
        function closeDelete() {
            document.getElementById('deleteOverlay').classList.remove('show');
        }
        setTimeout(() => {
            const t = document.getElementById('hcToast');
            if (t) { t.style.opacity='0'; t.style.transition='opacity .4s'; setTimeout(()=>t.remove(),400); }
        }, 4000);
    </script>
}

    <script>
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
                if (target) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    target.scrollIntoView({
                        behavior: 'smooth',
                        block: 'start'
                    });
                }
            });
        });
    </script>

@using WebBanHang_2380600870
@using WebBanHang_2380600870.Models
@addTagHelper *, Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.TagHelpers
// ===== FILE: C:\Users\Admin\source\repos\CoffeShop\WebBanHang_2380600870\Views\_ViewStart.cshtml =====
@{
    Layout = "_Layout";
}
// ===== FILE: C:\Users\Admin\source\repos\CoffeShop\WebBanHang_2380600870\Program.cs =====
// Program.cs â€” FIX: UseSession pháº£i Ä‘áº·t TRÆ¯á»šC UseAuthorization
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Identity;
using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using WebBanHang_2380600870.Models;
using WebBanHang_2380600870.Repositories;

var builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

// ===== DATABASE =====
builder.Services.AddDbContext<ApplicationDbContext>(options =>
    options.UseSqlServer(builder.Configuration.GetConnectionString("DefaultConnection")));

// ===== IDENTITY =====
builder.Services.AddIdentity<AppUser, IdentityRole>(options =>
{
    // DEVELOPMENT â€” password Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n
    options.Password.RequireDigit = false;
    options.Password.RequireLowercase = false;
    options.Password.RequireUppercase = false;
    options.Password.RequireNonAlphanumeric = false;
    options.Password.RequiredLength = 6;

    options.User.RequireUniqueEmail = true;

    // KhÃ³a tÃ i khoáº£n sau 5 láº§n sai
    options.Lockout.DefaultLockoutTimeSpan = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(15);
    options.Lockout.MaxFailedAccessAttempts = 5;
    options.Lockout.AllowedForNewUsers = true;

    options.SignIn.RequireConfirmedEmail = false;
})
.AddEntityFrameworkStores<ApplicationDbContext>()
.AddDefaultTokenProviders();

// ===== COOKIE =====
builder.Services.ConfigureApplicationCookie(options =>
{
    options.LoginPath = "/Account/Login";
    options.LogoutPath = "/Account/Logout";
    options.AccessDeniedPath = "/Account/AccessDenied";
    options.ExpireTimeSpan = TimeSpan.FromDays(7);
    options.SlidingExpiration = true;
    options.Cookie.HttpOnly = true;
    options.Cookie.SecurePolicy = CookieSecurePolicy.SameAsRequest;
});

// ===== SESSION =====
builder.Services.AddSession(options =>
{
    options.IdleTimeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(60);
    options.Cookie.HttpOnly = true;
    options.Cookie.IsEssential = true;
});
builder.Services.AddHttpContextAccessor();

// ===== REPOSITORIES =====
builder.Services.AddScoped<IProductRepository, EFProductRepository>();
builder.Services.AddScoped<ICategoryRepository, EFCategoryRepository>();
builder.Services.AddControllersWithViews();

var app = builder.Build();

// ===== SEED ROLES + ADMIN =====
using (var scope = app.Services.CreateScope())
{
    var services = scope.ServiceProvider;
    var db = services.GetRequiredService<ApplicationDbContext>();
    db.Database.Migrate();

    var roleManager = services.GetRequiredService<RoleManager<IdentityRole>>();
    var userManager = services.GetRequiredService<UserManager<AppUser>>();

    foreach (var role in new[] { "Admin", "User" })
    {
        if (!await roleManager.RoleExistsAsync(role))
            await roleManager.CreateAsync(new IdentityRole(role));
    }

    var adminEmail = "admin@goclang.vn";
    if (await userManager.FindByEmailAsync(adminEmail) == null)
    {
        var admin = new AppUser
        {
            UserName = adminEmail,
            Email = adminEmail,
            FullName = "Quáº£n Trá»‹ ViÃªn",
            EmailConfirmed = true
        };
        var result = await userManager.CreateAsync(admin, "Admin@123");
        if (result.Succeeded)
            await userManager.AddToRoleAsync(admin, "Admin");
    }
}

if (!app.Environment.IsDevelopment())
{
    app.UseExceptionHandler("/Home/Error");
    app.UseHsts();
}

app.UseStaticFiles();
app.UseRouting();
app.UseAuthentication();

// âœ… FIX QUAN TRá»ŒNG: UseSession PHáº¢I Ä‘áº·t sau UseAuthentication
// vÃ  TRÆ¯á»šC UseAuthorization â€” náº¿u Ä‘áº·t sau UseAuthorization,
// session sáº½ khÃ´ng khá»Ÿi táº¡o ká»‹p khi controller cáº§n Ä‘á»c giá» hÃ ng
app.UseSession();

app.UseAuthorization();

app.MapControllerRoute(
    name: "default",
    pattern: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");

app.Run();
